This link is broken. The target anchor does not exist or is commented out.
id=sign-up
The anchor after the # symbol points to a non-existent id on the target page. If the anchor link targets the same page nothing will happen when it's clicked. If the anchor link targets another page, then the top of the target page will be displayed instead of the intended location. In most cases the destination anchor has been removed accidentally and should be reinstated.

1068<div class="moduleVariation_moduleVariation__ctDqv moduleVariation_width__PJsO3 moduleVariation_spacingTop-80px__8K92x" style="--max-width:1320px;--width:91.66666666666666vw;--background:var(--white);--color:var(--black)">

1069<div class="moduleVariation_spacingBottom-100px__ztIzF">

1070<h3 class="h1 ModuleHeader_headerMain__gkAuX moduleVariation_spacingBottom-40px__CDK4M ModuleHeader_small__v4oVJ">

1071Our People </h3>

1072</div>

1073<div class="Default_copy__YVPrB">

1074<div class="StyledPortableText_styledPortableText__2iutY">

1075<h4 class="h4">

1076The core of our organizations success is the strength of our leadership, employees, and board members. Each plays a pivotal role in driving our mission forward and creating an environment where innovation and collaboration thrive. </h4>

1077<p class="p">

1078</p>

1079<p class="p light">

1080Our leadership team provides the strategic vision that guides us, ensuring we stay agile in a changing world while remaining focused on our long-term goals. Their ability to inspire and motivate not only directs our organizations path but also cultivates a culture where every team member can grow and succeed.</p>

1081<p class="p light">

1082</p>

1083<p class="p light">

1084Our employees are the foundation of everything we do. Their dedication, talent, and passion make a difference every day. We believe that each employee brings a unique set of skills and perspectives, contributing to a dynamic workplace where ideas flourish. By fostering a supportive and inclusive atmosphere, we empower our employees to reach their full potential, which in turn drives our organizations progress and enables us to better serve our stakeholders. Their hard work and commitment to excellence are what allow us to meet the challenges of today and anticipate the needs of tomorrow.</p>

1085<p class="p light">

1086</p>

1087<p class="p light">

1088Finally, our board members provide invaluable oversight and guidance, ensuring our organization remains on a path of sustainable growth. With their diverse backgrounds and wealth of experience, they offer strategic insights that help us navigate complex decisions and stay aligned with our core values. Their leadership fosters accountability, transparency, and innovation, reinforcing our commitment to making a positive impact. Together, our leadership, employees, and board members form a powerful team, driving our organization toward continued success and meaningful achievements.</p>

1089</div>

The CSS outline or border style on this element makes it difficult or impossible to see the link focus outline.
:focus and :not(:focus) have same outline:
Do not remove the default outline style, and change any border styles to avoid obscuring the focus outline around focusable elements. See :focus-visible for more information.

Using a border or outline style that obscures the focus ring causes problems for keyboard-only users in:

  • Chrome (obscures the focus indicator on links, buttons, dropdowns and range controls)
  • Firefox (obscures the focus indicator on links)

Line 2177 HTML5 ARIA 1.2

2177<div class="FooterPartners_partner__tkir8" aria-label=" ">

img elements must have an accessible name.
Add an alt attribute describing the image, which screen readers voice instead of the image. Spacer images and purely decorative images should use alt="" without any global ARIA attributes. Do not use alt text containing only spaces since that's voiced as an unlabeled image.

Impact on users:

  • NVDA 2023.3 Chrome 120 Windows 10 Reading: Image ignored.
  • NVDA 2023.3 FF 115 Windows 10 Reading: Image ignored.
  • NVDA 2023.3 Edge 120 Windows 10 Reading: Image ignored.
  • JAWS 2023.2311.34 Chrome 120 Windows 10 Reading: Image ignored.
  • JAWS 2023.2311.34 FF 115 Windows 10 Reading: Image ignored.
  • JAWS 2023.2311.34 Edge 120 Windows 10 Reading: Image ignored.
  • VoiceOver macOS 13.6 Safari 16.6 macOS 13.6.0 Reading: Image filename read out.
  • VoiceOver iOS 16.6 Safari iOS 16.6 iOS 16.6.1 Touch: Image filename read out, along with OCR text from image.
